Dai Ruzhao Executed 145

Principal Offender in the Murder of Huang Baoshan

Huang Baoshan, who operated a waste management business on Xiangyan Bridge Road in Hujiaqiao, was shot and killed a few years ago due to business jealousy. Following the incident, several people were apprehended and sentenced to lengthy prison terms or life imprisonment. The victim's family later apprehended Dai Ruzhao, a fellow villager who had previously worked as a detective in the Public Security Bureau, identifying him as the mastermind behind the crime. After the police station transferred him to the local court for review of previous case files, it was confirmed that Dai was indeed the principal offender and was wanted. Following the public prosecution, Judge Shen conducted multiple interrogations and debates. Yesterday, the proposal was submitted and Dai Ruzhao was sentenced to death for premeditated murder, and ordered to pay the victim's family, Wang Ji-shi, 3,650 yuan in consolation money and 300 yuan in damages. Dai Ruzhao protested the verdict, claiming innocence. The court ordered him to be taken down and held in custody pending further instructions.

On-site Examination of Two Deaths Caused by House Collapse 146

Due to a fire at No. 145 Aierkaoke Road, the homeowner hired plasterers Ye Sanmao and Zhang Hesheng to repair the remaining walls. The walls suddenly collapsed, severely injuring Ye and Zhang. They were rushed to Tongren Hospital for treatment. Zhang died from his injuries, and Ye also died last night from his injuries. The bodies were sent to the forensic examination center on Feilun Road. Yesterday morning, prosecutor Guo and forensic doctor Wei were dispatched by the First Special District Local Court to the center to examine the bodies. After confirming the cause of death, Wang Rongfu was summoned for questioning. He testified, "I was working in the same area that day, about 20 feet away from the deceased Zhang and Ye. Suddenly, I heard the sound of the wall collapsing, and the two of them were already buried in the rubble." The examination concluded that both Zhang Hesheng and Ye Sanmao died from injuries sustained before death due to being crushed. Zhang's body was handed over to his sister, Sun Zhang-shi, and Ye's body was handed over to his wife, Ye Gu-shi, to be taken back for burial.

Teenager Attempts Suicide by Poisoning Over Marriage Arrangement 147

At the Oriental Hotel near Xiaodongmen in Nanshi, a lone young man, wearing a blue-striped long gown, a felt hat, floral socks, and wool shoes, arrived at around 10:00 PM on the 19th of this month. He identified himself as Zhou Guxiong, 19 years old, from Ningbo. The hotel staff led him upstairs and opened room 33. Zhou entered the room to sleep. However, at 10:00 AM on the 20th, the guest had not yet gotten up. The waiter called out several times but received no response, nor did he hear any movement from inside the room, which seemed strange. He then went to peek through the cracks in the wall of the adjacent room and saw the guest lying horizontally in bed, with the bedding in disarray and a pale face. Realizing something was wrong, the waiter immediately reported to the front desk, and they managed to pry open the door to the room. Upon inspection, they found several pieces of paper resembling opium wrappers on the floor, indicating a suicide attempt by poisoning. The hotel manager, Chu Lianke, reported the incident to the Second Precinct of the First District Public Security Bureau. The precinct chief, Bao Bingchen, dispatched police officer Gong Weichuan to investigate. It turned out that the hotel had already sent the poisoned guest, Zhou Guxiong, to the Nanshi Public Hospital for treatment. After examination by Dr. Jiang Zhenxun, it was determined that the poisoning was too severe and his life was in danger. According to the doctor, the person was not actually named Zhou. A relative surnamed He came to visit and revealed that his real name was He Zigui, 18 years old, residing on Xinzha Road and working at a customs brokerage in Shanghai. The reason for the suicide was his mother's arrangement of his marriage. It is said that the poison he took was sleeping pill powder.

Attention Telephone Users 156

Beware of Swindlers

Recently, a Chinese man in his late twenties or early thirties, about five feet seven inches tall, of medium build, with a slightly dark and round face, large and round eyes, short hair, wearing a blue cloth short jacket and trousers, and a checkered duckbill cap, has been swindling people out of their telephones. He speaks fluent English and targets residential and commercial establishments. His methods are particularly innovative. The swindler often claims to be an employee of the telephone company and inspects telephones under the pretext of inspection. After the inspection, he claims that the telephone needs repair, dismantles various components, takes them away, and says that he will return to reinstall them soon. However, he disappears like a yellow crane, and neither he nor the telephone are ever seen again. When questioned, the swindler produces a paper certificate with his photo and the number 107, so people do not suspect him. Many people have been fooled recently.

Educational News - Important News

Ministry of Education Orders Jiangsu Education Department to Temporarily Suspend Changing Names of Experimental Schools 161

The Jiangsu Education Department decided to convert seven schools, including Zhenjiang Middle School, into normal schools, stop enrolling ordinary students from this semester, and rename the seven experimental primary schools, including Zhenjiang Experimental Primary School, as affiliated primary schools. This was reported in the previous newspaper. Representatives of teachers and staff from Jiangsu Experimental Primary School, including Yu Gancheng, opposed changing the experimental primary schools to affiliated schools and submitted their opinions to the Ministry of Education, requesting them to instruct the Jiangsu Education Department to withdraw the order to change the names and maintain the original experimental primary school system. After receiving the submission, the Ministry of Education, believing that the points raised were not without reason, issued an instruction to the Jiangsu Education Department yesterday (June 20) stating: "Recently, the Jiangsu Provincial Experimental Primary School Teachers and Staff Representatives, including Yu Gancheng, submitted a report to the Ministry stating that the Jiangsu Provincial Experimental Primary Schools have been changed for five years. At the beginning of the change, the significance was extremely important. Now, the Jiangsu Education Department is abolishing a part of it and changing it to an affiliated name. The colleagues of the Vocational School held a meeting in Zhenjiang on the 12th of this month and unanimously decided to request the Jiangsu Education Department to withdraw the order and to request Your Excellency to instruct to maintain the original experimental primary school system. According to the presentation, there are currently a total of fifteen Jiangsu Provincial Experimental Primary Schools. Now, because seven middle schools will be converted into completely independent normal schools within two years, the seven experimental primary schools will be changed to affiliated primary schools of the middle schools in advance. Firstly, it is not necessary to change the name of the primary schools before the normal schools become independent. Secondly, after two years, they will be changed to affiliated primary schools of a certain normal school, and the names will be changed frequently. Thirdly, for the same primary school, those that provide practice for normal school students are called affiliated primary schools, while those that do not provide practice for normal school students are called experimental primary schools. The names are ambiguous, and the system is inconsistent. After investigation, the points raised are not without reason. It seems necessary to reconsider the entire plan and temporarily suspend the renaming. However, since it concerns local education, the department should report the handling process and its opinions for record."

Representatives of Jinan University Faculty and Staff Arrive in Beijing to Demand Overdue Salaries 163

·Minister Zhu's Reply·

Full Salaries to be Paid from July

Back Pay Must Await Entire Plan

On the afternoon of the 20th, five representatives of the faculty and staff of Jinan University, Xie Xunchu, Yu Jitai, Chen Kemei, Gu Ming, and Zhang Feng, arrived at the Ministry of Education to demand overdue salaries. Zhu Jiaju met with them. The representatives requested three points: (1) to pay the full three months of overdue salaries for November, December, and January; (2) to make up the 60% of salaries for February, March, and April (40% has been paid), and 50% of salaries for May and June; and (3) to pay the faculty and staff salaries in full from now on. Zhu replied that from July onwards, the funds for all national schools would be allocated in full. After the funds were allocated in full, the Ministry of Education would negotiate a repayment plan with the Ministry of Finance for the overdue funds. The existing 30% and 50% of funds were not intended to write off the unpaid funds. The Ministry of Education only stated that the receipt of a certain percentage of funds was to retain the possibility of demanding the remaining unpaid funds. However, this method was a predetermined arrangement by the government as a whole, and it was not aimed at education funds alone. The Ministry of Education did not seem to be in a position to propose a separate compensation plan, etc. The representatives expressed only partial satisfaction with what Zhu said and would report back to the entire faculty and staff at the school for discussion on further salary demands. It is heard that the representatives will go to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance on the 21st to continue their petition.

Jinan University Faculty's Declaration to the Ministry of Education and Ministry of Finance Demanding Salaries Since the professors and others at Jinan University began attending classes in March of this year, enduring pain and suffering, they have proposed salary demands at two dinners in April and early May. At that time, they all believed that since foreign disasters were raging and military needs were urgent, those who held educational positions should be concerned about the country and have public-minded loyalty. Therefore, they repeatedly stopped discussing this matter. However, they still hoped that as time passed and the situation changed, the ruling officials would definitely understand the difficulties of the people and issue their life-sustaining salaries in advance, without having to demand them. However, under the leadership of "long-term resistance, the whole plan," we resist every day but retreat every day, and we negotiate every day but agreements are made. Classes have been held for four months, and summer vacation is just around the corner, but the salary that we need and cherish is nowhere to be found. It is tolerable to have the salaries for life-sustaining teaching positions delayed and ignored, but it is intolerable! Resistance is long-term, and we do not know when it will end. Planning is holistic, but local instability is already causing great turmoil. After repeated forbearance and deliberation, we were forced to convene our colleagues and held a salary demand meeting at the First Academy of our school on Hede Road at 4:00 PM on June 15 to discuss effective methods. In the end, we all agreed to elect representatives to draft a report and set out for Beijing on the 19th of the month to demand overdue salaries from the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Finance. In the report, the main requests were: (1) Please pay the full amount of the three months of overdue salaries for November, December, and January of last year. (2) Please pay the deducted percentage of salaries for the four months of February, March, April, and May of this year. (3) Please pay the full amount of school funds from June onwards. (4) Please issue the temporary funds of 230,000 yuan that were previously approved and allocated. The report also stated clearly, "We hope that the government will accommodate the above four items. If there is no satisfactory response and sincere acceptance, we will have no choice but to take concerted action within the scope permitted by the school regulations to arouse the sympathy of the national education community and to promote the government's attention." Now that the representatives are on their way, the government's sincerity is at stake, and the future of education depends on this. We hope that the representatives will work hard and ask for the assistance of the national education community. This declaration is hereby made for your public consideration.

To be Held in Hangzhou in September

With the national crisis intensifying and foreign insults becoming more urgent, economic issues are of utmost importance. The Chinese Economic Society, recognizing this, plans to gather experts at this year's annual meeting to discuss national crisis economic issues. Dear Sir, The Society intends to discuss the economic problems of the national crisis at this year's annual meeting. The discussion time is planned to be limited to four hours each time. First, three or four people will be responsible for reading papers and expressing opinions in turn (each limited to forty minutes), and then three or four people will be responsible for commenting (each limited to ten minutes), in order to stimulate the spirit of debate and achieve the effect of mutual learning. The annual meeting is scheduled to be held in Hangzhou in September. Please identify all paper and comment topics before June 6 of this year and inform us in advance so that the Paper Committee can collect, arrange, and consult again to assign responsibilities. Enclosed is a draft outline of the economic problems of the national crisis to be discussed at the annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society for your reference. Please provide further details and suggestions for discussion. We would be very grateful. The draft outline of the national economic crisis to be discussed at the annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society is attached. The first discussion will address the relationship between China's national crisis and the world economy. The second discussion will address the economic problems in the national crisis and their solutions (note that the word "various" can be added above the economy). The topics for the third and fourth discussions are the same as above. President Ma Yinchu, member of the Paper Committee, Li Zhaobao, correspondence address: Shanghai Jiaotong University, etc.

Recording of Striking the Temple Bell (3)(10) The Unkempt Scholar Doesn't Remove the Courtyard Grass 165

Thirty-three

I said: "Mr. Zhu wants me to be a senior disciple, which I am quite willing to do. But it's just that I will teach others what I know, and learn from others what I don't know. It doesn't seem necessary to distinguish between senior and junior. As for the master's chair, please, sir, sit down honestly and without ceremony, there's no need to decline."

Mr. Zhu said: "Broadly speaking, not only are there no senior or junior disciples, but even the distinction between master and disciple cannot be clearly drawn. Take me for example. I can be your master in some things, but I need to be your disciple in others. Not to mention anything else, just take the matter of striking the bell, I should be apprenticed to you. Not only should I apprentice to you, there are few people in the world who wouldn't need to apprentice to you."

Mr. Zhu's words struck a chord with me. Which young person doesn't like to hear compliments? I knew that Mr. Zhu certainly wasn't trying to plant seeds of pride in my heart. He was just using a simple example to prove that there are no strict boundaries between teacher and student. However, I must be careful not to let people's compliments about the small matter of striking the bell lead me to actually put on the airs of a master. Even if I become a master in the future, I must still be willing to humbly be a student, only then will there be hope for progress. I agree with Mr. Zhu's idea of running a school like Han Xin commanding troops, the more the better. But I don't quite agree with recruiting one-year-old infants. In the end, I had to honestly raise my concerns: "Sir, you should reconsider recruiting infants. You see, after these infants arrive, crying, being held, being hungry, urinating, defecating all day long, you'll have to take care of everything yourself, how can you manage? If you ask the senior disciples to help, who would be willing?"

Mr. Zhu said: "You don't have to worry about that, I have ready-made disciples. These disciples are each infant's own mother. By teaching each mother, we are teaching each infant." I said: "This also has its difficulties. The customs in our village are not enlightened. Sir, how can you, a man, properly instruct women? Once there is suspicion of impropriety, it won't be a small matter."

Mr. Zhu said: "It's always acceptable for women to teach women, right? I think Old Mrs. Song is quite good. If she is willing to come out and lead, are there still problems? There shouldn't be any gossip if we help her, right?" I said: "That's safer. But why is Sir in such a hurry to start with infant education?" Mr. Zhu said: "If a child's emotions, habits, and tendencies are not properly cultivated before the age of six, it will be difficult to change them in the future. For example, fear of ghosts is a most unreasonable emotion, almost entirely created by women's rumors. And the result? Fear of ghosts when young, fear of ghosts forever. How important is education before the age of six! Therefore, to cultivate elementary school students, we must first cultivate kindergarten students, even more so, we must cultivate infants, that is, we must cultivate the mothers of infants, that is the fundamental approach. Wanting to run an elementary school well without paying attention to mother education is like trying to catch the moon in the water, how is it possible?"

Free Talk

The "Eating the Party" Comrade in the Child's Mouth 181

The effectiveness of the word "eat" is very broad. Doing what kind of business is called eating what kind of food: gambling stall owners hope to eat everything, socializers are only afraid of losing face; others, like students, after every exam, privately discuss who will definitely eat an A, who will definitely eat a B, eat a C, eat a D.

Eating religion is different from believing in religion. If you call someone who believes in religion "eating religion," that person is sure to object. Who would have thought that, in addition to "eating religion," there is now also the term "eating the Party." The person who created the term "eating religion" doesn't refer to faithful believers, but to those who use religion to beg for food. By analogy, all the characters who "eat the Party" are probably not faithful Party members, but are just using the Party to beg for food; I think that the Party must not have any characters who "eat the Party" in order to maintain the Party's dignity and remain unchanged over time.

A friend told me a new joke:

In a certain province, there was a faithful comrade named Jiang Mian. It is not certain whether these are the exact characters; anyway, it's just a joke, so let's just write two characters at random.

After Jiang Mian joined the political party, he worked hard for the Party, and was definitely not a person who relied on the Party for food. One day, Jiang Mian was passing through a small alley, when he heard the children inside shouting: "Jiang Mian, a comrade who eats the Party! Jiang Mian, a comrade who eats the Party!"

Hearing this, he couldn't help but feel angry. He was a faithful comrade, what kind of kids! How dare they call him by name and call him a comrade who eats the Party!

He angrily ran inside, intending to negotiate with those kids; but, after investigating, he couldn't help but laugh; it turned out that the kids were reading the Analects, and what they were reading was: "Que dang tong zi jiang ming! Que dang tong zi jiang ming!" (A boy from Que dang was delivering a message!)

The Bamboo Hat of the Nineteenth Route Army 182

— Eternal Remembrance

This time, the bamboo hat of the Nineteenth Route Army not only gave the Japanese a permanent and profound understanding, but also gave the people of the world an understanding. The Japanese have recently published a book called "Photographs of the Nineteenth Route Army," which also uses a bamboo hat as an advertisement, which shows that after receiving a great lesson from the Nineteenth Route Army, they firmly recognized this bamboo hat. Perhaps later they will feel that the bamboo hat is a thing to be feared, hated, and respected!

Many foreigners think that the bamboo hat is a specially made military hat of the Nineteenth Route Army, thinking that it can also protect against bullets like foreign steel helmets. Even many Chinese people have the same view. In fact, this kind of bamboo hat is a very popular hat among farmers in Guangdong, especially farmers in Zhongshan County. Men and women wear it when they go out, whether it is sunny or rainy. They call it a "copper drum hat." Each hat costs only twenty or thirty cents. It can protect against the sun and also shelter from the rain. It is made of two layers of fine bamboo, with palm leaves sandwiched in between. After buying a hat, most farmers write their names on it, and then spend three or five cents to add a layer of cooked tung oil, which makes it brighter and more durable. (There are people in the market who specialize in carrying loads of cooked tung oil, making a living by oiling hats for people.) Two straps are added to the inner edge of the hat. When worn, the straps are tightened so that the wind won't blow it off. When not in use, the straps are loosened and hung on the back, which does not hinder work at all. It is cheap, durable, and serves multiple purposes, and can be regarded as a blessing for farmers in Guangdong. The Nineteenth Route Army likes to use it, probably because they are mostly from Guangdong, and also because it is a practical thing. Wearing it on the heads of hardworking farmers can give them comfort, and wearing it on the heads of patriotic soldiers can give the enemy a great lesson and enhance our international status. Bamboo hat! We will always love you! (No remuneration received)

Overseas Chinese Rarely Get to Raise Their Eyebrows 183

— Stone

I recently received a letter from a friend studying in the United States, saying that since the January 28th Incident in Shanghai, our army's good news has been constantly transmitted to the United States. Major and minor newspapers across the country have used large-print headlines to report the news of the Chinese army resisting the enemy. Not to mention that our overseas Chinese compatriots in the United States are all elated, even the just people of the United States are all inspired and energized, praising the Eastern Sleeping Lion for stretching and awakening. One evening, my friend gathered dozens of friends and took a seat in a cafe to discuss supporting the military affairs of resisting Japan in Shanghai. A novelist at the next table learned that these dozens of overseas Chinese were discussing national salvation and donations, and suddenly requested to give a brief speech. My friend allowed it. The novelist immediately stood up and spoke, with many encouraging words. Among them, there were several sentences that said: If we see two people fighting in the street, we must come out and mediate, because if two strong people fight, one of them will definitely be injured. Once one is injured, they will definitely seek revenge in the future, so there will inevitably be no day of peace. If a strong person fights a weak person, and the strong person violently beats the weak person, and the weak person does not resist, then the strong person can be allowed to beat the weak person to death, so there will be no fear of future troubles. Japan occupies Northeast China, and China retreats without resistance, which is a fight between the strong and the weak. Today, the Japanese army invades Shanghai, and the Chinese army resists with all its strength, which is a fight between two strong people. We, the people of the United States, should urge the government to intervene and must not stand idly by. I deeply hope that the Chinese army in Shanghai will resist to the end, then the great powers will definitely come out and help China to achieve success. From this, we can also see that the greatness of the Shanghai gunshots has crossed the Pacific Ocean and awakened the Americans. One day, my friend was eating in a small eatery. Several Americans at the next table were talking boastfully about the Battle of Shanghai, with many derogatory remarks about the Japanese. Later, seeing my friend, they mistakenly thought he was Japanese, so they all offered comfort. My friend quickly told them that he was not Japanese, but a respectable Chinese. They then rushed to shake hands with my friend and raise their glasses to toast, such was their opportunism. Although the above two incidents are just minor anecdotes, from this we should always remember this glorious and great Battle of Shanghai. Because our overseas Chinese have never been respected by people when residing abroad. This is the first time in decades that they have been able to speak out and raise their eyebrows.

Strange Fish 185

— Gao Qian

Among fish, there are many strange ones.

Climbing trees to catch fish: Mencius said to King Xuan of Qi, "To do what you are doing to seek what you want to get is like climbing trees to catch fish." It means that climbing trees to catch fish is impossible. Unexpectedly, there are actually fish in the world that climb trees. This kind of fish is produced in East India. It can use the small hooks outside its gill covers to climb tree trunks.

Electric fish: Humans have worked hard and spent the thoughts and efforts of many scientists and engineers to create generators. But unexpectedly, there is a kind of fish in nature that can automatically release electricity without any effort. This kind of fish is produced in the rivers of South America and Africa.

Flying fish: Birds can fly and fish can swim. This is a fact that everyone knows. But conversely, it is also possible to say that birds can swim and fish can fly. Passengers taking ships from Shanghai to Europe and the United States can often see flying fish on the ocean.

Bullet-shooting fish: There is a kind of fish in East India that can spit out water droplets from its mouth to knock insects into the water, which is similar to the sword heroes described in our country's novels who spit out white light from their mouths.

Lantern fish: At the bottom of the deep sea, sunlight cannot reach it. It is truly what is called "the sky is wrong and the earth is dark, the sun and moon have no light." Fish living here can emit their own light to guide them in the darkness.

Fish in a dried-up pond: Although the pond is dried up, some fish may not die. The lungfish produced in Africa usually swim in the water. When it is dry and the water dries up, it hides in the mud, breathing air and living.

New Armament Spectrum (Middle) 186

— ·Tie·Mi·Tuo

Modified Anti-Aircraft Gun: The modified anti-aircraft gun was invented by Dai Hongbin, the commander of the armored vehicle unit of the Third Route Army. It was modified from a 29-fold Creusot field gun with a caliber of 7 centimeters. It is installed on a specially made steel armored vehicle's dome-shaped gun platform. The top is made of steel rails, and people stand below it to operate it. It is easy to use. Its range is 75 degrees in the air and 7,300 meters in height. The projectile is shrapnel. The shell is divided into ten layers, each layer containing 18 bullets. The explosion force reaches 20 meters in width and 70 meters in length. It was tested in Jinan.

Flying Mine: The flying mine was invented by Cai Linsheng. Cai is also a factory member of the Northeast Arsenal. The flying mine is a kind of automatic elliptical projectile. The body is 70 centimeters long. The medicine cylinder is 50 centimeters long and its caliber is 30 centimeters wide. It was first tested in Shenyang. It flew as high as 1,000 meters. It was then tested in Xindu. The power was slightly inferior, but it also reached over 800 meters. The explosion force reached 60 meters. When it reaches a considerable height, it can also explode on its own. This year, when the Japanese pirates invaded Shanghai, on February 13th, it was reported that it was used to resist the bandits. It shattered a bandit plane at the Sun Temple.

Rocket: The rocket was invented jointly by Guo Liquan and Zhao Jiulong. Both gentlemen are also factory members of the Northeast Arsenal. The rocket is a modification of the flying mine. The only difference is that the degree of repair only reaches one-fifth. The caliber is also smaller. The range is the same as the flying mine.

On Wang Shaolou's Soul-Stealing Bell 187

— Liu Huogong

Wang Shaolou's arrival in Shanghai this time has been extremely well-received by audiences. His performance skills are indeed excellent. However, from my perspective, the "Soul-Stealing Bell" is the most unique and interesting. This play of his uses the method of singing old plays with new arrangements. The opening scene uses the "Returning Dragon Pavilion," with the phrase "changing clothes inside the Dragon and Phoenix Pavilion" from "Return Dragon Pavilion," followed by a "xipi daoban" (a type of musical interlude in Peking Opera). Then, he sings the "xipi yuanban" (a main melody in Peking Opera), which is Yang Yanzhao from "Beheading the Son" descending the stage to welcome his mother. "Visiting Mother" is like a wild goose from the south losing its flock and scattering. "Nanyang Pass" sighs that parents cannot help but shed tears like pearls. "Pearl Curtain Village" recalls the Five Phoenix Tower of yesteryear. "Celebrating Top Pearl" laments that his family is poor and has no means. "Reporting a Strange Injustice" says that in an instant, dark clouds cover the sky. "Fa Men Temple," the villain Liu Jin, has a general's head hanging high on a pole. Then, he explains that Pigsy has been ordered by the Monkey King to explore Lion Camel Ridge. Because the road is long and he is tired, he sings opera to relieve boredom. He then sings three segments from "Teaching the Son," Wang Chun'e's "Old Xue Bao, you don't need to plead bitterly..." Xue Bao's "Advise the Third Lady to stop shedding tears..." and Chun'e's "You say he is young, but he is not small..." He plays both the male and female roles and sings in rapid succession. The audience finds it enjoyable, but it must be tiring for the performer. The following is the "Yi Tune," "Returning Boat in the Wind and Rain," sung very much in the style of Chang Shutian. Then, he performs the sword dance from "Farewell My Concubine." The dance is personally taught by Mei Lanfang, so it is naturally exceptionally captivating. After the dance, he does two "hawk flips" and lies straight down. He gets up and walks the flower steps, then uses a "da mian" (painted face) voice to sing the "xipi duo ban," the original lyrics of stealing the bell from passing through the Black Cloud Cave. Later, he sees the female character (the female lion) making a humorous explanation, which is also very interesting. Then, he steals the fake bell and fights with the demons, showing off the iron rake. He sees the Earth God and has another long humorous explanation. Then, he transforms into a small Pigsy and finally follows the Monkey King to the double-advance formation, performing the "banchao tian deng diao mao" (a challenging acrobatic move). It is done very lively. Then, the beautiful monkey comes up and drags him down by the waist. Only then is the play finished. The soul-stealing bell of ordinary actors is not sung like this. That's why I say it's particularly interesting. "If you don't believe me," please go see it for yourself.

Record of Ma Shuanglou (86) 188

— Master of Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter 10: Powerful Officials Bully and Oppress, Fortunately, a Lady Provides Comfort; Shortcuts and Bribes Achieve Advancement, Commanding Generals Anew, Mountain Bandits Enlisted

The on-duty clerk, with a forced smile on his face, slightly nodded to An Yutian. This was considered a complete act of courtesy, barely expressing gratitude. Then, he took a business card, raised it high with his hand, and gestured towards the door, saying, "Please." An Yutian hurriedly said goodbye to Wan Jinsheng and entered the large reception hall. He glanced inadvertently at both sides and saw the same scene as yesterday, with many scholars solemnly and silently present. However, he had now ascended to the sky and would no longer be relegated to the position of a petrified exhibit. He couldn't help but feel a sense of the past and present and strangely thought of these poor people sitting there bored. It must be that he had such a virtuous wife to plan for him, so he didn't have to endure this kind of bitter task every day. He then felt very happy and pitied those people very much. From the clerk's office door, he turned to the back and entered a second gate like an iron threshold. Two armed guards stood watch. The clerk said, "Without their guidance, no one can enter here, except for the most prestigious incumbent division commanders and the main leaders of this office." An Yutian gratefully accepted the favor and paid solemn respect. After passing through a large courtyard, there was a row of tall houses facing him. Four guards with hand-held submachine guns stood in formation on the steps. He walked into the house and went straight to the easternmost room, which was Military Governor Ye's signing room. Many people could not easily step into it even after waiting for a year or two. However, things in the world are difficult when they are said to be difficult, and easy when they are said to be easy. The clerk only opened the doors and windows and announced inside that Councilor An had arrived. He didn't even need a card. An Yutian entered with fear and trepidation. Ye Zuozhang was wearing a military uniform and sitting on a swivel chair behind a large desk. He glanced at An Yutian and waved with a smile. An Yutian bowed quickly and stood beside the desk. Ye Zuozhang opened his mouth and asked, "Has your wife come?" An Yutian replied that she was at the hotel. Ye Zuozhang then said, "She can come to the office to play often." As he spoke, he happily swayed his small body in the chair. Then, he talked about whether the hotel was convenient or not. An Yutian then boldly presented a memorial requesting approval to recruit troops. Ye Zuozhang readily picked up a pen and wrote an approval, appointing An Yutian as the recruiting commissioner, with a deadline of one month to complete the task. After inspecting the weapons and personnel, he would be assigned a military position. He pointed to an officer wearing a lieutenant general's epaulette on the opposite chair and said to the chief of staff, "Let him handle this official business." An Yutian was overjoyed and bowed to both sides to express his gratitude. Then, others came to see Ye Zuozhang to talk. An Yutian retreated to the side and carefully examined the room's decorations. He saw walls full of photographs and mirror frames, and a few pairs of couplets personally written by the current president and prime minister. There wasn't much to see, so he quietly walked out and hurried home to report the good news. To know what happened next, please read the next chapter.

Shen Bao Local Supplement, Wednesday, June 22nd, Year 21 of the Republic of China

(No Additional Charge)

Discussion

If You Don't Understand the Law 201

— Buddha

The lack of clarity in legal provisions often leads to misunderstandings between judges and parties involved. There are numerous examples of this, and I cannot discuss them all individually. Let me just give one example.

According to yesterday's newspaper, I was surprised to read about a case where a spouse was not allowed to file a private prosecution for bigamy. I am not someone who has studied law and naturally don't understand its intricacies. However, from a logical and emotional standpoint, the reason for not allowing private prosecution is truly incomprehensible.

It is said that Article 339 of the Code of Criminal Procedure explicitly states this. The article reads, "The provisions of the preceding two paragraphs do not apply to lineal relatives, spouses, or relatives living under the same roof." Indeed, this article clearly states that spouses cannot file a private prosecution. However, the simple provision does not explain why. It seems that the legislator's intention is that such cases concern national legal interests or violate public morals and must be prosecuted by the public prosecutor.

However, Article 340 of the Code of Criminal Procedure states, "If the same case has been privately prosecuted, it cannot be reported to the public prosecutor or judicial police officer again." If these two articles are interpreted together, it seems that all cases must be requested to be prosecuted by the public prosecutor. If the case has already been privately prosecuted, it cannot be reported to the public prosecutor or judicial police officer again. There is no provision that the court absolutely cannot accept private prosecution. If we consider only Article 340, it says that if a case has been privately prosecuted, it cannot be reported to the public prosecutor again. This clearly refers to public prosecution cases. If a case has already been privately prosecuted, a request cannot be made to the public prosecutor again to avoid double prosecution. The reasoning is clear.

The crime of bigamy is one that directly and most painfully affects the spouse. Originally, lineal ascendants should have the right to report the crime. However, under the system of freedom of marriage, parents naturally don't interfere in their children's affairs. Therefore, private prosecution is the only recourse. So, if the spouse doesn't come forward to report the crime of bigamy, should uncles and cousins do it?

But the law says that bigamy cases must be requested for public prosecution. However, in the special circumstances of the concessions, such cases are commonplace. I don't know if the courts reject all of them or accept some and reject others. If they are all rejected, then victims of bigamy committed in the concessions will naturally have no way to seek redress. This is unreasonable from an emotional and logical standpoint. If it is said that the Municipal Council must be requested to initiate prosecution, that is even more incomprehensible. What was the point of the government's relentless efforts to regain jurisdiction over the concessions? Now, Chinese citizens are pushing away lawsuits between Chinese citizens, requiring them to seek help from the Municipal Council. I truly don't understand.

The iron lock of Wusong snaps a thousand fathoms, fragrant trees and slanting sun, half the forest red. Li Guang enters the mountain with lonely indignation, Qu Yuan loves to sing and walk by the Ze. Born at the wrong time, I grieve for Geng Xin, the trees are still like that, I am filled with regret for Huan Wen. From ancient times, battles end with death, the majestic mountains and rivers respect the Dao. Countless insects and sands return to the Kalpa, wanting to pour a cup of wine to mourn the loyal souls.

Science

The Use of Three Types of Meters 204

— Yuting

Electricity is a versatile thing and an indispensable element in the world. In this era of thriving electricity, we must utilize it and know its essence. At the very least, we should have common sense of electricity. Now, I will write down the names of three important meters in electricity and their uses:

(1) Ammeter (Ａｍｐｅｒｅｍｅｔｅｒ) (2) Voltmeter (ＶｏｌｔＭｅｔｅｒ) (3) Ohmmeter (Ｏｈｍｍｅ)

Ammeters are used to measure current. Voltmeters are used to measure voltage (or potential difference) and electromotive force. Ohmmeters are used to measure resistance.

After Ohm's research, he discovered that the magnitude of resistance is inversely proportional to current and directly proportional to potential difference. Assuming V is the potential difference, A is the amount of current, and R is the magnitude of resistance, we can establish the following formula:

V

R=-

A

Knowing the above formula, we can use the laws of algebra to list the following two formulas:

V

A=-　　V=AR

R

The above three formulas were created by Ohm, so we call this law Ohm's Law.

A Corner of Society

The Pastime of Shanghai Ladies 205

— Ying Dai

The day before yesterday, my younger brother and I bought some things at Sincere Department Store and returned home. Passing through an alley, two children suddenly approached, holding a stack of leaflets printed with lead letters. Smiling, they handed each of us one. I usually hate being given leaflets and never accept any on the street. However, seeing that these two children were young, lively, and innocent, I was prompted by curiosity to find out the purpose of their leaflets. I only took a look, but it would have been better if I hadn't. It made me laugh. The leaflet read:

"A stone tablet of Liu Bowen has been discovered in a certain place. This year, China will be in great chaos. Certain provinces will experience floods, certain provinces will experience wars, and certain provinces will experience plagues..."

In short, according to this leaflet, no part of China will be spared this year. Below were some nonsensical sentences, nothing more than:

"First worry, there is food but no one to eat; second worry, there are clothes but no one to wear; third worry, there are roads but no one to walk; fourth worry..."

"Fifth worry..." and so on, up to the tenth worry.

Below were also three magical talismans, said to prevent disasters if drawn on the door. If everyone could print and distribute these leaflets, doing good deeds would dispel misfortune and prolong life. Otherwise, nine out of ten people would die this year, and even chickens and dogs would not be spared.

Walking past, I found the same leaflets pasted on the walls at the alley entrance. After a few days, there were more and more leaflets. Every time we went out, people would hand them out, and the walls of the alley were covered with them. Before long, Mrs. Zhang next door, Mrs. Li across the street, and so on, were all asking people to print these leaflets for distribution.

Nonsense like "In a certain month this year, the world will be in chaos and darkness" and "In a certain month, there will be mass deaths" can often be heard and are not worth a scholar's laugh. But some old ladies believe these messages to be true, telling everyone and inquiring everywhere. As a result, besides verbally advising people to be good, they also print and distribute leaflets.

Originally, the ladies of Shanghai have nothing to do all day after eating their fill. Sitting at home, they feel bored. With these rumors, they have something to talk about. At the same time, they are panicked, as if a great disaster is imminent. As for distributing leaflets, the wealthy ladies naturally don't care. The poor ones may even save money to print leaflets. This is also a pastime for Shanghai ladies.

While the ladies are rushing to print and distribute leaflets, the printing shops are having the best luck.

Learning to Write

Students Testing the Teacher 206

— Yiyi Guan Zhu

The day before yesterday, I met my old friend Mr. Zhao, whom I hadn't seen for many years. Of course, we exchanged recent updates. I asked him, "I haven't seen you for a long time. What have you been up to lately?" He said, "Nothing special, just working as a teacher in a small elementary school." I said, "Being a teacher is very leisurely, unlike me, who makes a living with a pen and ink, constantly working on documents all day without a moment of free time!" He said, "Being a teacher is indeed relatively leisurely, but sometimes it's not easy. When you encounter mischievous students who play tricks, there's nothing you can do. They often look up strange, obscure words or uncommon allusions in the dictionary to ask me. If the teacher can't answer immediately, they'll mock him. Isn't that embarrassing?" I laughed and said, "That's what you call 'Zhang Tianshi possessed by a ghost, having magic but no way to use it!'" He laughed too, and we shook hands and parted in laughter.

When I returned home, Mr. Zhao's words reminded me of when I was a child, studying in a small elementary school in my hometown (Huzhou). The Chinese teacher was a scholar with a solid foundation in Chinese classics. One day, after he had finished explaining a lesson, he told everyone to read the lesson again because it was still early before the end of class. If there was anything they didn't understand, they could ask him. Then a certain student, nicknamed "Old Year Flowered Eagle," who was notoriously mischievous, didn't read the text but looked up words in the dictionary. He found the three characters "錫," "茶," and "壼" in the dictionary and wrote them down to ask the teacher, saying, "What are these characters?" The Chinese teacher said to that student, "Don't you recognize these three characters? They are "雪," "查," and "胡," which is a tin teapot." The student then pretended to be serious and said, "How come I just looked it up in the dictionary, and these three characters are called Yang, Tu, and Kun. I was still a little confused, so I wrote them down to ask the teacher. Now that the teacher says "these three characters are pronounced "雪," "查," and "胡," which is a tin teapot," then it must be the dictionary's mistake." The Chinese teacher, hearing the student say this, carefully looked at the three characters "錫," "茶," and "壼" again. It turned out that each character had an extra stroke compared to the characters "錫," "茶," and "壼." If he hadn't consulted the dictionary, he really wouldn't have recognized them. At that time, I saw the Chinese teacher's expression, truly embarrassed and laughable! This is what Mr. Zhao was talking about, "students testing the teacher," inevitably embarrassing the teacher.

Business Skills

Busy 207

— Zaichang

Talking about business, Mr. Xi vividly described a doctor, saying,

Once, because there was a patient at home, it was inevitable to ask a doctor to take a look. As for famous doctors, a large amount of money is required to get them to "look up to" or "condescend," otherwise "the rich man's gate is as deep as the sea," and you can only be "Xiao Lang is a passerby." If you want them to "come quickly," it's even more difficult. No matter how anxiously the patient is like an ant on a hot pot, waiting until his neck is as long as a luffa, he still arrives late. That's how famous doctors are. Then the only choice is not to consult them. Fortunately, the patient has a minor illness, so it's better to ask a doctor who lives nearby and isn't famous and whose practice is deserted. First, the price is cheap, and second, it's easy to ask and they arrive quickly. Once the decision was made, it was immediately carried out. Satisfyingly, within half an hour, he could "condescend to visit." Who knew that three hours passed and still no sign of him? Suspicions made me wonder if he was popular now? Was business busy? Finally, he did come. The doctor came! I saw him panting and running, his face red. From his own announcement, I learned that he had just examined a patient somewhere and had only now arrived here. He hastily looked at the patient, hastily wrote a prescription, and from his own announcement, he had to go to another consultation elsewhere. So I saw him leave very hurriedly. After the doctor left, I thought, "Even bricks and tiles have their day to turn over." A doctor who had previously been unasked for had suddenly become popular.

A few days later, a friend of mine who was familiar with that doctor came to talk to me. Unintentionally, we talked about that doctor. I asked him,

"Do you know how he suddenly got lucky, and business has become so busy?"

"Where did you hear that?" my friend asked me.

So I told him this story. Unexpectedly, my friend burst out laughing at me, then said,

"You also fell into his trap. This is his advertising plan, completely a business tactic."

Living in a Dream

Electric Rabbit 208

— I

The movie had been going on for half the time. During the ten-minute intermission, several young artists from the same art group were sitting in a row, waiting for the "superbly beautiful and world-renowned European female star Anna Antler starring, supremely interesting and wondrous construction of Speedy First Kiss (Anny Onkrain; All for Kiss'" to continue playing.

The beauty of this film is just as the theater advertised, "Completely bringing the unrestrained attitude of Western women to the screen, with unexpected wonders..." This is highly praised by Mr. A, who advocates extreme freedom in love. He even dared to compare the female lead in the play to Miss Wu, whom he admired. So he called out in the typical tone of a poet:

"Ah! This is simply a portrait of our Angel! How realistic it is."

"Our Miss Wu? Oh! No, Old A, you can't insult her like that. What reason do you have to curse her?" Little Chen, who calls himself a playwright and has the nickname "Wild Dog," spoke in pure Mandarin as if reading lines.

"That's right, it's really unreasonable. Just because she doesn't love you, do you have to insult her personality?" The beautiful novelist was simply angry. Old A then added:

"Who says so? She doesn't love me? I'm the one who's ignoring her."

"I'm afraid that's not the case?" The young artist chimed in. "She is so beautiful, with rosy cheeks and deep red, dripping lips. Who wouldn't be moved by her? If I didn't already have a lover, I would fall in love with her."

"That's right, who doesn't know? Chasing her like a dog all day long, who can you hide it from?" "Wild Dog" said again. So Old A became angry out of embarrassment and even cursed out loud.

"Bullshit! You're the real wild dog!"

At this time, the vocalist, Tao Shao, who was on the far right, suddenly raised his loud voice and said:

"Everyone doesn't need to say anything. You are all dogs running in the dog track, desperately chasing the electric rabbit in front. Whoever has the highest stake will run in the front, but the electric rabbit can never be caught. It's just a waste of effort."

"........"

Suddenly, the lights went out, and the beautiful girl appeared in front of them again, so everyone had to concentrate on dealing with this current illusion.

Being a Traitor for Five Minutes 209

— Hong

Old classmate Mr. T came to school to see me. As soon as he sat down, he said to me with a smile:

"I was a traitor for five minutes! I tasted the flavor of being a traitor!" Who did? A traitor, a traitor! Are they divided into five minutes or ten minutes? I couldn't help but ask him in surprise. After I asked him, he told the whole story from beginning to end.

"When I walked to Zhonghongqiao, just about to get on the bridge but not yet, more than thirty armed soldiers from ×× walked horizontally. The sentry patrolmen had already placed their wooden sticks horizontally, and I couldn't break through their path, so I had to stop. The one in the lead, with a red border on his hat, was probably the captain. He thought about me, slightly lifted his hat, and said in very awkward Shanghai dialect.

"Where to go to Honganji (Nishi Hongwanji)?"

Of course, I explained to him that it was on Wuchang Road and indicated it with gestures. He pointed at me with his hand, meaning he wanted me to be a guide. At that time, I had no choice but to walk, so I had to guide him forward. However, the eyes of my compatriots on the road were all on me, clearly thinking that I was a traitor. Although I was innocent, I couldn't help but blush. I also really admitted that I had become a traitor, but it only lasted for five minutes, so I said I was a traitor for five minutes."

Automobile News - Essays

The Small and Capable British Austin - Dan Hua 213

Generally, pioneers and visionaries must undergo a period of intense struggle and declare war on fate before they can achieve success and shine through the ages. Civilization gains a step forward, and humanity gains a bit more happiness. It is indeed a gift from those with foresight and vision.

Affordable and rapid transportation is a modern treasure, and Lord Austin, the pioneering founder of this field, occupies a prominent position. His invention, the Austin Seven, is like a revolutionary army in the automotive world, now popular everywhere and becoming a necessity.

The Austin Seven is a pioneer among small cars. Its high capabilities and widespread popularity have exceeded the inventor's expectations.

The Austin Seven was not specifically designed as a racing car, but it surpassed its peers in the 1923 Italian Grand Prix and won the first prize. The following year, it set nineteen records for 750cc class cars. It also won prizes and honors in various European countries.

In 1926, it participated in the Australian 632-mile race. Despite the extremely difficult conditions, it triumphed, which is particularly commendable. It also set three records in Brooklands.

The following year, it set even more records at Montlhéry, from three hours to five hundred miles. In 1928, it set five more records at the same location, reaching as high as twenty-four hours.

In the following year, it distinguished itself both domestically and internationally, especially in Northern Ireland and South Africa.

1930 was the year the Austin Seven set new records in New Zealand and South Africa, and it also won the Double Twelve race.

Recently, Mrs. Souter drove an Austin Seven at 110 miles per hour and set four international records. Such are the achievements of the Austin Seven in the racing world.

In other aspects, the Austin Seven, with its solid construction and exquisite design, is fearless in the face of adversity. Anyone who has driven it is amazed by its great capabilities.

The Austin Seven was the first car to drive to the top of Table Mountain.

The Austin Seven was the first car to ascend and descend Ben Nevis in one day.

The Austin Seven was the first car to be driven around the world by a woman.

The Austin Seven was the first car to be driven solo across Europe to Cairo, Egypt.

The Austin Seven was the first car used in polar expeditions, enduring intense pulling every day.

The Austin Seven was the first car to reach Cape York in Queensland.

The Austin Seven is the first 750cc car to drive the measured miles and kilometers at a speed of over 100 miles per hour.

From the above, it can be seen that even in the worst weather or road conditions, sometimes with no roads at all, the Austin Seven can reach everywhere and overcome dangers with ease.

Facts are the greatest debaters. Any further words would be gilding the lily.

Alarming Number of British Vehicle Accidents - Pei 214

Eighteen People Die Under Wheels Every Day

London Dispatch. Recently, the Minister of Transport, Mr. Pybus, and other government officials in charge of traffic management, declared that road accident cases in Great Britain are increasing daily, causing widespread public anxiety. According to Mr. Pybus's report to the House of Commons, in 1931, 6,691 people in England died in road accidents, and 200,219 were injured as a result. The magnitude of these numbers is truly astonishing.

In 1931, the total number of British people who died, were disabled, or injured due to vehicle accidents was 208,810. This exceeds the number of British soldiers killed, wounded, and lost to disease in the Boer War by more than four times. Such a huge number of casualties in a single year of peace is truly noteworthy. These statistics were released during a meeting of the National Safety Council and during National Safety Week. The National Safety Council discussed various accident events related to transportation and industry.

The traffic accident casualty rate averages eighteen deaths and 533 injuries on the nation's roads every day. Comparing the statistics of 1930 and 1931, there were 614 fewer deaths in 1931, but 24,224 more injuries. In the London area alone, 27,977 traffic accidents occurred in the first three months of this year, resulting in 314 deaths and 10,865 injuries. Among the dead, 224 were pedestrians, 20 were car owners, 40 were cyclists, and 24 were motorcycle drivers.

During the National Safety Council meeting in the United Kingdom, the Secretary-General of the Ministry of Transport, Mr. Bickerdike, gave a speech, stating that the majority of accident events can be reduced by preventive measures. For example, if a plague were to break out in the country and the number of deaths were similar to that of these vehicle accidents, then all medical professionals in the country would immediately rise up and urgently seek preventive medicines.

[>Image caption: Citroen car chassis before assembly.

The situation of assembling the car body and cushions inside the Javel factory.

Page 20

As for preventing vehicle accidents, stricter penalties are needed. It is also necessary to awaken public judgment and impose adequate penalties on reckless drivers who cause the loss of others' lives.

Regarding the causes of vehicle accidents, generally speaking, in cities, the blame lies with pedestrians, while in the countryside, drivers should be held responsible. This is generally accepted by the public. In the first three months of this year, 224 people in London, England, died under vehicles, of which the police blamed 163 for negligence. This is because those from the countryside often do not pay attention to traffic control, which leads to this. Therefore, since London started using automatic traffic lights, car drivers have become more cautious, while pedestrians have become careless, crossing the streets at will.

Regarding car accidents in the countryside, according to the Royal Automobile Club, the blame should be attributed to both parties. Accidents occur when they pass each other in places with poor visibility or are careless when turning. Also, when entering a main road from a side road, if the view ahead is unclear and one is not careful, a major disaster can occur. As for careless pedestrians in bustling cities, the only way to deal with them is to impose severe penalties to remind them. Furthermore, cyclists who arbitrarily weave through traffic should be severely punished.

Although vehicle accidents in the United Kingdom in 1931 were 614 fewer than in 1930, 1931 was a year of economic recession, and the number of registered cars decreased by 3.2 percent, so the number of accidents also decreased by 8.5 percent. Traffic accidents in London in 1931 were 73 fewer than in 1930. According to Mr. Bickerdike, this is because there were fewer deaths of motorcycle drivers and passengers on London streets last year. He also said that the use of motorcycles as a means of transportation in London has decreased compared to before.

A prosthetic leg dealer once told a correspondent for the New York Speaking Platform newspaper that since the end of the war, his largest customers have been those injured while driving motorcycles.

French 24-Hour Automobile Grand Prix 215

Havas Agency, Le Mans, France, 19th. The 24-hour automobile Grand Prix ended at 4 pm today. The Italian Alfa Romeo car came in first. The drivers of the car were Sommer and Chinetti. The car traveled 2,954 kilometers and 038 meters, with an average speed of 123 kilometers and 084 meters per hour. The second place was also an Alfa Romeo car. The drivers were Gaudet and Chinetti. The car traveled 2,914 kilometers and 272 meters. The third place was a D'Arleau car, driven by Lewis and Lechard. The car traveled 2,428 kilometers and 560 meters. When the race started, there were 26 cars. Only three French cars, three British cars, and three Italian cars reached the finish line.

Advantages of the Williams Overrun 216

The 113-inch wide wheelbase of the Williams Overrun six-cylinder car now makes the car's driving more stable, and its extended hood further enhances the car's length and grandeur. Therefore, from a practical point of view, everything from the V-shaped water tank to the rear of the car is well-proportioned. This new car has truly opened a new era of the highest standard of beauty for the company's low-priced six-cylinder cars. What is particularly commendable is that this new design is further enhanced by the harmony of various colors, the exquisite and luxurious velvet brown cushions, and the neat and elegant stripes, which complement each other and are extremely beautiful. As for the car body styles, there are five-seater sedans, five-seater small sedans, two-seater coupes, four-seater coupes, two-seater roadsters, four-seater roadsters, and sedans. All of these styles are extremely spacious and exceptionally comfortable. Being inside is no different from being at home. The front seats of the car can be moved forward or backward at will. The backrests of the front seats inside the sedan can also be adjusted at will to suit individual needs and achieve extreme comfort. In addition, the steering column can also be adjusted at will.

Miscellaneous Records

Overview of the Citroen Factory - Fu 217

The Citroen factory is the most important automobile manufacturer in Europe. Its rapid progress and its reputation throughout the country are all due to the excellence and superiority of its manufacturing work, which is unmatched. As for its ability to produce large quantities at the lowest possible cost, it must be attributed to the excellence of its machinery, the adoption of scientific methods, and the meticulous and thoroughness of all its manufacturing management. When the first 14-horsepower Citroen car was launched, it was in 1919. At that time, only 30 cars were produced per day. Since then, the production volume has increased with each passing day. At the beginning of 1927, the daily production volume reached more than 400 cars. However, compared with today, there is still a huge difference, because the current daily output has more than doubled compared to 1927. The Citroen factory is now divided into many locations. It employs 25,000 people, uses 40,000 horsepower, 15,000 pieces of excellent and sophisticated machinery, and 33,000 inches of conveyors and assembly lines. As for its manufacturing work, whether large or small parts, it is constantly striving for excellence and perfection. The factory has its reasons for its achievements today; it is not by chance.

Overview of Highways in Henan Province (Continued) Black Fox 218

Road maintenance methods. Roads are built with the original intention of facilitating public travel and the United Motors Company. Recently, another large batch of German Oberle four-cylinder and six-cylinder cars has been shipped in. There are also many specially prepared new cars to welcome people from all walks of life to come and try them out. The picture above is a photo of the Oberle new car in front of the company's gate.

Page 21

. If road maintenance methods are not properly planned, allowing vehicles to press on the road and rainwater to wash over it, the roadbed will inevitably collapse and the road surface will crack before long. Therefore, the issue of road maintenance is as important as road construction. The entire territory of Henan, except for the southwestern parts with many mountains, is mostly plains with no end in sight. Road construction is relatively easy compared to other provinces, but maintenance is actually more difficult than in other provinces. The reason is that the soil quality in various places mostly contains sand and has extremely poor cohesion, making it difficult to solidify. Therefore, the roadbed and road surface are eroded by wind and rain and crushed by vehicles, and will collapse before long. Moreover, for thousands of years, the only means of transportation relied upon in Henan Province has been large carts. These carts are made in two types: two-wheeled and four-wheeled. The wheels are wrapped with iron skin. Once loaded, when traveling on the road, the road surface is pressed into deep ruts. Although the provincial government has repeatedly advocated improving the manufacturing methods of large carts and opening large cart roads outside of automobile roads to allow them to travel separately to avoid crushing, the result has been inconvenient. The manufacturing methods remain the same and have not been changed. Avoiding what is difficult and seeking what is easy is human nature. All drivers of large carts want their carts to travel on car roads. Although imperial proclamations are issued and strict penalty rules are established, it is difficult to prohibit them. Therefore, in order to protect the roads, the Henan Provincial Highway Bureau has formulated measures to divide important highways according to the counties they pass through, and assign one member of the local militia and autonomous region residents to guard every ten li. This kind of measure does not increase provincial funds and does not increase the local burden, so it has been implemented in various counties. As for the existing public automobile business on various roads, a budget is being formulated separately to set up road maintenance teams, with one person for every ten li. Currently, a road maintenance team has been established for the Kaixu section, with one team leader and 20 road maintenance workers. Road maintenance teams for other sections, such as Kaizhou and Kaikao, will also be established one after another.

Status of Traffic Operation. Examining the long-distance automobile transportation business in Henan Province, it has not been well-developed in the past. In the 18th year of the Republic of China, in order to facilitate transportation, the Provincial Department of Construction began to vigorously promote and formulate regulations to encourage merchants to run long-distance automobile companies, and ordered eight cars from foreign firms to be operated by the Highway Bureau to promote the official automobile business. However, it stopped operating shortly after starting due to political changes. All the cars were almost completely lost, leaving only two broken cars that could not be driven. In the winter of the 19th year, when the transportation situation stabilized, the Department of Construction again submitted a request to the provincial government to allocate funds to order 20 Chevrolet cars from the Anli Foreign Firm in Hankou. The Department then organized a long-distance automobile business department and actively prepared for traffic (1) The Kaixu Line (Kaifeng to Xuchang) used new cars and changed to simultaneous departures from Kaifeng and Xuchang stations. There were four round trips per day. Various regulations were also formulated, and ticket sales on the bus were abolished and replaced with ticket sales at each station. All management was very strict, and the bus timetable was also very accurate. A total of five stations were set up: Kaifeng, Zhuxianzhen, Weishi, Youchuan, and Xuchang. Passengers along the line can purchase tickets and take the bus at nearby stations according to the scheduled times, which is very convenient for travelers. The business at Kaifeng and Xuchang stations is very good, followed by Weishi and Youchuan stations. Zhuxianzhen station is relatively inferior. (2) The Kaizhou Line (Kaifeng to Zhoujiakou) This line is an important road in southeastern Henan Province, with a large number of travelers coming and going. Originally, it was a commercially run automobile business for transportation, but the vehicles were dilapidated and could not be driven, and the timetable was uncertain. Once the car engine was damaged, it could not arrive until the next day. After the new cars were put into operation, it took about six hours to reach 350 miles, and it could be a round trip in one day. Chenliu, Qixian, Taikang, Huaiyang, Zhoujiakou, and other places along the line are all important towns. Setting up stations to sell tickets, the business income is the highest on this line. (3) The Kaicao Line (Kaifeng to Caozhou) There are four stations along the line: Quxing, Jikaocheng, Caikouzhen, and Caozhou. This line is actually an important road connecting Shandong Province, so the business is gradually developing, and travel is also convenient.
